Grand Prix Memphis Day 2 Archetype Decklists
============================================



 Posted in [COVERAGE ARCHIVE](/en/events/coverage)
 on February 22, 2015 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20170709072651im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/themes/wiz_mtg/images/global/generic-avatar-150.png)
By Adam Styborski and Peter Rawlings










With so many archetypes appearing in Day 2, we decided to feature as many as we possible could! If you took a peek at the metagame breakdown and wondered what that deck looked liked, you can get a taste of it here. Enjoy!
